Alternatively, you&#39;re welcome to email us if that suits you better. We&#39;re here to help!</p><ul id="buttons01" class="style1 buttons"><li><a href="https://discord.gg/S6ZJuFnXje" class="button n01"><svg><use xlink:href="#icon-3b7eeeccbb457780f277fce4669f67a0"></use></svg><span class="label">Join our discord</span></a></li><li><a href="mailto:support@getnotable.ai" class="button n02"><svg><use xlink:href="#icon-c3c8e1063e3b7f84f6b54712741de139"></use></svg><span class="label">Send us email</span></a></li></ul><h2 id="text01">User FAQs</h2><p id="text76" class="style15">Overview of Notable</p><p id="text07" class="style13">What is Notable?</p><p id="text43" class="style12"><span class="p">Notable empowers you to effortlessly summarize, import, export, save, share, vote, and explore key takeaways, from anywhere.<br /> <br></span></p><p id="text58" class="style13">How can I benefit from Notable?</p><div id="list02" class="list"><ol><li><p><strong>Instant and accurate takeaways</strong>. Notable distills main points from a lengthy content (talks, lectures, podcasts, tutorials, etc.). Notable integrates with OpenAI, so you get accurate takeaways in just few clicks.</p></li><li><p><strong>Easy takeaway capture and import</strong>. You can effortlessly capture pre-written key points in slides, posts, comments, ChatGPT answers, handwritten notes, and more. Import them in seconds, so and can manage them a one place.</p></li><li><p><strong>Retain key learnings</strong>. You can save your takeaways, or bookmark other users&#39; takeaways, for quick access later.</p></li><li><p><strong>Free knowledge at your fingertip</strong>. You can access curated learnings from assorted sources, in clear, digestible formats.</p></li><li><p><strong>Seeking collective wisdom</strong>. You can gain top valuable learnings and insights, shared and resonated by masses, so you grab the best gems.</p></li><li><p><strong>Boosting your influence</strong>. You easily export and share your top insights in crisp and beautiful format that your social network love to read.</p></li></ol></div><p id="text56" class="style13"><br>How does Notable work?</p><p id="text46" class="style12">At Notable, users <em>create</em> and <em>consume</em> takeaway notes. A <strong>note</strong> is a collections of concise <em>key points</em> distilled from an original source.</p><div id="list05" class="list"><ul><li><p><em><strong>Creating notes</strong></em>: Users capture, save, and publish their takeaways in the form of <em>notes</em>. While many rely on AI assistance to generate these takeaways, they can also import pre-existing insights or input them manually.</p></li><li><p><em><strong>Consuming notes</strong></em>: Users read notes to quickly grasp the essence of the sources. They can further engage with these notes by liking or bookmarking a note, starring an individual key point, sharing, and more.</p></li></ul></div><p id="text73" class="style12"><strong>Think of notes like posts on Instagram</strong>. Just as a picture captures a thousand words, a note condenses volumes of information into bite-sized insights.</p><p id="text83" class="style15"><br>Getting the App</p><p id="text47" class="style13">How do I access Notable?</p><p id="text49" class="style12"><span class="p">Simply download our iOS app from the App Store. We&#39;re working on Android.</span><span class="p">Alternatively, you can access our web app on your mobile browser by visiting https://getnotable.ai.</span><span class="p">If you are interested in a web app optimized for desktop, you can show your support by upvoting this feature on our Discord channel.</span><span class="p"><br></span></p><p id="text14" class="style13">Is Notable available outside U.S.?</p><p id="text08" class="style12">At this moment, the Notable app is only available on the U.S. App Store. We are working on expanding to other countries soon. You can show your support by upvoting your country&#39;s store on our Discord channel.</p><p id="text84" class="style15"><br>Creating Your Account</p><p id="text85" class="style13">Do I need a Notable account to use Notable?</p><p id="text86" class="style12"><span class="p">Yes, most features of Notable requires a Notable account. It&#39;s simple though: you can sign up with Google, or with email and password.</span><span class="p">That said, reading a note is possible without an account. For instance, if you have a link to a note like https://getnotable.ai/n/NSk9hVfnyF, you can open this link in your browser and read the note, even without being logged in. You can also share the link to your friends, and they can read it right away without signing up.</span></p><p id="text91" class="style13"><br>How can I create an Notable account?</p><p id="text92" class="style12"><span class="p">After your download the app, press the &quot;Get Started&quot; button. Click the &quot;Sign up&quot; link.</span><span class="p">Press &quot;Continue with Google&quot; to sign up a Notable account with your Google account. Alternatively, you can sign up with your email and password for Notable.</span></p><p id="text93" class="style13"><br>What is &quot;Display Name&quot; of my Notable profile? How to update it?</p><p id="text94" class="style12"><span class="p">Your Display Name is what other users will identify you in notes you created.</span><span class="p">You can set it to whatever name you like. It allows spaces or characters in other languages. It has a limit of maximum 20 characters.</span><span class="p">Multiple users may have the same names, so you may choose something that represents you or stands out.</span><span class="p"><strong>To update your Display Name:</strong><br /> 1. Click on the <em>Account</em> tab button.<br /> 2. Click the <em>Settings</em> icon on the top right corner.<br /> 3. Click the <em>Profile</em> menu item.<br /> 4. Click the <em>Name</em> item.<br /> 5. Enter your desired name.<br /> 6. Click confirm.</span></p><p id="text33" class="style13"><br>What is &quot;Profile Picture&quot;? How to update it?</p><p id="text34" class="style12"><span class="p">The &quot;Profile Picture&quot; is the image that represents you on our platform. It&#39;s the visual identifier associated with your account, making your interactions and contributions easily recognizable to other users. Multiple users may have the same picture.</span><span class="p">Today we support choosing from avatars as your profile picture. If you want to upload your own picture instead, please upvote feature in our Discord channel.</span><span class="p"><strong>To update your Profile Picture:</strong><br /> 1. Click on the <em>Account</em> tab button.<br /> 2. Click the <em>Settings</em> icon on the top right corner.<br /> 3. Click the <em>Profile</em> menu item.<br /> 4. Click your <em>Profile Picture</em>.<br /> 5. Choose your desired avatar.<br /> 6. Click confirm.</span></p><p id="text77" class="style15"><br>Managing Notable Credits</p><p id="text37" class="style13">Do I have to pay to use Notable?</p><p id="text38" class="style12"><span class="p">No, most features are free. This includes searching, viewing, and bookmarking other users&#39; takeaway notes, as well as creating and sharing your own notes.</span><span class="p">However, the &quot;Summarize with AI&quot; features do require credits. This helps Notable cover the costs associated with providing high-quality summaries from OpenAI.</span><span class="p">In the case of summarizing video, every 10-min video requires 1 credit. In the case of summarizing article or text, every 5000-character requires 1 credit.</span><span class="p"><br></span></p><p id="text35" class="style13">Do I get free credits as new users?</p><p id="text36" class="style12"><span class="p">Yes, new user who signs up will receive 20 free credits. That&#39;s good for summarizing 200 minutes of videos (e.g., good for 10 videos if each is under 20 mins).<br /> <br></span></p><p id="text39" class="style13">What is the pricing for Notable credits?</p><div id="list06" class="list"><ul><li><p>20 credits pack for $2.99 (~$0.15/credit)</p></li><li><p>60 credits pack for $7.99 (~$0.13/credit)</p></li><li><p>180 credits pack for $19.99 (~$0.11/credit)</p></li><li><p>540 credits pack for $49.99 (~$0.09/credit)</p></li><li><p>Currency are USD.</p></li></ul></div><p id="text40" class="style12"><span class="p">You might notice higher price per credit for smaller packs. This is because the relative costs associated with processing small transactions are high. As the pack size increases, these transaction costs are spread out, allowing us to offer a more competitive price per credit.<br /> <br></span></p><p id="text55" class="style13">How do I buy Notable credits?</p><p id="text71" class="style12"><span class="p">Log in to Notable for iOS, go to Account tab. Click &quot;Reload Credits&quot; button, and following the on screen instruction. The purchased credits will instantly reloaded to your account after successful purchase.</span><span class="p"><br></span></p><p id="text41" class="style13">Do you offer subscription based pricing?</p><p id="text42" class="style12"><span class="p">We are working it. We want to make sure you are getting great premium features and value out of our subscription plans.</span><span class="p"><br></span></p><p id="text29" class="style13">Without credits, can I still get a YouTube video summarized?</p><p id="text30" class="style12"><span class="p">Yes. If you&#39;re out of credits and cannot reload, you still have some options:</span><span class="p">1. Find existing notes for the video. Many popular contents will have notes already created by the community.</span><span class="p">2. Invite a friend to join. They will get free credits to help with your request. Ask them to share you the link to the note containing the takeaways.</span><span class="p">3. Join our Discord server and ask the community to summarize the video for you. They can share with you the link to the note.</span><span class="p"><br></span></p><p id="text82" class="style15">Creating and Editing Notes</p><p id="text74" class="style13">How to create a note?</p><p id="text90" class="style12"><span class="p">The most important part for creating a note is to prepare the list of takeaways. We offer flexible ways for you to prepare the list.</span><span class="p">Press the &quot;+&quot; button on the bottom the screen, which will open a menu. Select from one of the below options:</span></p><p id="text72" class="style12">By summarizing long contents into takeaways with AI:</p><div id="list07" class="list"><ul><li><p><strong>Summarize <em>online video</em></strong>. You can input a video URL. AI will analyze video, pinpoint key moments, and generate concise takeaways.</p></li><li><p><strong>Summarize <em>online article</em></strong>. You can input an article URL. AI extracts takeaways. The article can be SNS post, blog post, or a generic web page.</p></li><li><p><strong>Summarize <em>any text</em></strong>: Similarly, you can copy paste in arbitrary text content, such as specific section of lengthy doc or email.</p></li></ul></div><p id="text75" class="style12">By importing existing takeaways:</p><div id="list08" class="list"><ul><li><p><strong>Import from <em>photo</em></strong>: You select a photo, and Notable recognizes the key points inside the photo. When you see a useful list of pre-written takeaway in a post, an offline presentation slide, a handwritten memo, a ChatGPT answer, simply take a picture, or a screenshot. Notable will handles the rest.</p></li><li><p><strong>Import from <em>text</em></strong>: Similarly, you can copy paste in a list of pre-written takeaways, and Notable can auto import them. Those takeaways might be written in digital docs, emails, posts, a YouTube comment, a ChatGPT answer (if copy pasting text works better than snapping).</p></li></ul></div><p id="text32" class="style12">By entering takeaways directly:</p><div id="list03" class="list"><ul><li><p><strong>Type in</strong>: You can always type in takeaways directly from their mind. Ideal for when sources are offline contents or personal experience.</p></li></ul></div><p id="text50" class="style13"><br>Can I keep my notes private on Notable?</p><p id="text54" class="style12"><span class="p">Yes. We support <em>Private Notes</em>. They are not <em>discoverable</em> by other users and are not <em>viewable</em> even if other users have the direct link to the notes.</span><span class="p"><strong>How to make a note private?</strong><br /> 1. When creating or editing a note, click on the Visibility option.<br /> 2. Choose <em>Private</em>.<br /> 3. Save your note. It&#39;s now set to private mode!</span><span class="p"><strong>One thing to remember:</strong><br /> If your note was initially public and someone bookmarked it, that note&#39;s title will still appear in their bookmark list. However, they won&#39;t be able to access its contents if you later switch it to private.</span></p><p id="text27" class="style13"><br>Can a note be accessible by only me or anyone who I share a direct link with?</p><p id="text16" class="style12"><span class="p">Yes, we support <em>Unlisted Notes</em>. They are not discoverable by other users, though they are accessible if other users have the direct link to it.</span><span class="p"><strong>How to make a note unlisted?</strong><br /> 1. When creating or editing a note, click on the Visibility option.<br /> 2. Choose <em>Unlisted</em>.<br /> 3. Save your note. It&#39;s now set to unlisted.</span><span class="p"><strong>Remember:</strong><br /> Just like with private notes, if your note started off as public and was bookmarked by someone, its title will remain in their bookmark list. If you later change its visibility to unlisted, they&#39;ll still be able to open and view its contents through their bookmark, much like the other users have manually recorded the direct link to your note.</span></p><p id="text81" class="style13"><br>How do I summarize an online video?</p><div id="list01" class="list"><ol><li><p>Press the + button on the bottom the screen, which will open a menu.</p></li><li><p>Press &quot;Online Video&quot; button, under the &quot;Summarize contents into takeaways&quot; section.</p></li><li><p>Follow the on screen instruction.</p></li></ol></div><p id="text80" class="style12"><span class="p"><strong>YouTube videos only</strong><br /> Today we only support videos (including video shorts) on YouTube. In you need supporting videos on other platforms, join our Discord channel to upvote the feature.</span></p><p id="text26" class="style13"><br> Why did I get this error: &quot;We could not summarize this video, due to no caption in any language found for video...&quot;?</p><p id="text45" class="style12"><span class="p">Today we only support videos with at least one subtitle/transcript (of any language). Notable relies on the subtitles to understand the video content.</span><span class="p">While most English-speaking video has at least the auto-generated English subtitle, non English-speaking videos may not have any subtitle.</span><span class="p">In you need supporting videos without subtitle, upvote the feature on our Discord channel.</span></p><p id="text79" class="style13"><br>How do I summarize an online article?</p><p id="text78" class="style12">Press the + button in the bottom of the screen which will open a menu. Press &quot;Online Article&quot; button, under the &quot;Summarize contents into takeaways&quot; section. Follow the on screen instruction.</p><p id="text59" class="style15"><br>Reading and Engaging Notes</p><p id="text44" class="style13">What are the different ways of consuming notes?</p><div id="list04" class="list"><ul><li><p><strong>Find a note</strong>: You can search notes by the URL of the content (e.g., a YouTube video). Popular videos may already have notes created by other users.</p></li><li><p><strong>Read a note</strong>: You can skim through the takeaway headings, and can deep dive into specific takeaway details. Use Focus Mode for full-screen, distraction-free reading experience.</p></li><li><p><strong>Sort takeaways</strong>: You can sort the takeaway points inside a single note by the timestamp, starred count (voted by the community), or by Notable Score.</p></li><li><p><strong>Watch video and jump to moments</strong>: You can watch the source YouTube video inside the app, and jump to the timestamp of a takeaway instantly.</p></li><li><p><strong>Bookmark a note</strong>: You can bookmark a note, which allows you to save it for future reference.</p></li><li><p><strong>Like a note</strong>: You can express your appreciation for a note by liking it, which serves a feedback for the note creator and the community.</p></li><li><p><strong>Star a point</strong>: Within a note, you can &quot;star&quot; specific key points. This serves a feedback for the note creator and the community.</p></li><li><p><strong>Share a note</strong>: You can share notes with their social networks, spreading knowledge beyond the Notable app. You can also post notes back to the original content platform, assisting wider audience there.</p></li></ul></div><p id="text24" class="style13"><br>How to find existing notes for a YouTube video?</p><p id="text25" class="style12">Go the the second tab, paste in the YouTube video URL. Then click the &quot;Search notes for content at URL&quot; button.</p><p id="text09" class="style13"><br>What are different ways of sharing a note?</p><div id="list09" class="list"><ul><li><p>Copy the note link.</p></li><li><p>Copy shareable pre-formatted takeaways text.</p></li><li><p>Download sharable pre-formatted images.</p></li></ul></div><p id="text48" class="style12"><span class="p">You can then share the link, text, or images to your friends or in your social network.</span><span class="p">Join our Discord and share your thoughts on you would want to share a note.</span><span class="p"><br></span></p><p id="text31" class="style13">How do I bookmark a note?</p><p id="text22" class="style12"><span class="p">Inside the note detail page, press the bookmark icon on the bottom. You can find all of bookmarks inside the Library tab.<br /> <br></span></p><p id="text87" class="style13">How do I star a point?</p><p id="text88" class="style12"><span class="p">Inside the note detail page, press the star icon of the given point. Staring a point indicates you find the point particularly useful or interesting.</span><span class="p">If you&#39;d like to have the points you have starred shown up in your Library, feel free to upvote the feature in our Discord.</span></p><p id="text19" class="style13"><br>How do I report a note?</p><p id="text51" class="style12">If you come across a note that seems inappropriate, misleading, or violates our terms of service, please take the following steps to report it:</p><div id="list10" class="list"><ol><li><p>Navigate to the specific note you want to report.</p></li><li><p>Look for the &#39;Options&#39; or &#39;More&#39; button (usually represented by three dots or an ellipsis) near the note title or at the bottom of the note.</p></li><li><p>Click on it and select &#39;Report Note&#39; from the dropdown menu.</p></li><li><p>You&#39;ll be prompted to provide a reason for the report. Choose the one that best describes your concern or add details in the provided text box.</p></li><li><p>Click &#39;Submit Report&#39; to finalize your report.</p></li></ol></div><p id="text89" class="style12">Our team will review the reported note promptly and take appropriate action based on our guidelines. Thank you for helping us maintain the integrity of our platform!</p></div></div></div></section><section id="tos-section"><div id="container06" class="container default full screen"><div class="wrapper"><div class="inner"><p id="text52">Notable Terms of Service</p><p id="text53"><span class="p">Effective Date: 8/30/2023</span><span class="p">Welcome to Notable, a platform designed to help you discover, distill, share, and remember key takeaways from various digital content, live experiences, or your personal knowledge.
